# English to Concilium: Paragraphs

## Paragraph 1

English: One friend asked another if they wanted to go hiking on Saturday. The other checked their schedule and said it sounded like a great idea. They started planning the route and what supplies they should bring. Soon the plan turned into a small adventure.

Concilium: midra tsesel rur raeskror melmom rir krovakh gaekh shelle drilaer lalri rasha. shor shaer ludros narla drirlin vun dris merdo dan lartle sheslukh shusha shem. rir shava minlakh shor khor vun sho me rir dron mutlol. gemkha shor sholser dreda di sheslukh nir lessha.

Pronunciation: [m-ee-dr-ah] [ts-eh-s-eh-l] [r-oo-r] [r-eye-s-kr-oh-r] [m-eh-l-m-oh-m] [r-ee-r] [kr-oh-v-ah-kh] [g-eye-kh] [sh-eh-l-l-eh] [dr-ee-l-eye-r] [l-ah-l-r-ee] [r-ah-sh-ah]. [sh-oh-r] [sh-eye-r] [l-oo-dr-oh-s] [n-ah-r-l-ah] [dr-ee-r-l-ee-n] [v-oo-n] [dr-ee-s] [m-eh-r-d-oh] [d-ah-n] [l-ah-r-tl-eh] [sh-eh-s-l-oo-kh] [sh-oo-sh-ah] [sh-eh-m]. [r-ee-r] [sh-ah-v-ah] [m-ee-n-l-ah-kh] [sh-oh-r] [kh-oh-r] [v-oo-n] [sh-oh] [m-eh] [r-ee-r] [dr-oh-n] [m-oo-tl-oh-l]. [g-eh-m-kh-ah] [sh-oh-r] [sh-oh-l-s-eh-r] [dr-eh-d-ah] [d-ee] [sh-eh-s-l-oo-kh] [n-ee-r] [l-eh-s-sh-ah].

## Paragraph 2

English: A man nervously asked his date what kind of music she liked. She smiled and said she enjoyed many different styles. They discovered they both liked the same old band. That small coincidence made the conversation easier.

Concilium: sheslukh gelra shorshal rur drunshir rokro sho dral tlunta gogar mendi ver. mendi ga vun dris mendi nonres taskren munshokh laesni. rir laem rir lon ver shor dre drornikh num. dak nir le raere shor lor sinro.

Pronunciation: [sh-eh-s-l-oo-kh] [g-eh-l-r-ah] [sh-oh-r-sh-ah-l] [r-oo-r] [dr-oo-n-sh-ee-r] [r-oh-kr-oh] [sh-oh] [dr-ah-l] [tl-oo-n-t-ah] [g-oh-g-ah-r] [m-eh-n-d-ee] [v-eh-r]. [m-eh-n-d-ee] [g-ah] [v-oo-n] [dr-ee-s] [m-eh-n-d-ee] [n-oh-n-r-eh-s] [t-ah-s-kr-eh-n] [m-oo-n-sh-oh-kh] [l-eye-s-n-ee]. [r-ee-r] [l-eye-m] [r-ee-r] [l-oh-n] [v-eh-r] [sh-oh-r] [dr-eh] [dr-oh-r-n-ee-kh] [n-oo-m]. [d-ah-k] [n-ee-r] [l-eh] [r-eye-r-eh] [sh-oh-r] [l-oh-r] [s-ee-n-r-oh].

## Paragraph 3

English: Someone on the bus asked the passenger next to them if the seat was taken. The passenger moved their bag and said it was free. They both nodded politely and looked out the window. The bus continued moving through the busy streets.

Concilium: li lalri shor tlisla rur shor segem tsimon gaekh khekhnil melmom shor drem drelaes shekhraes. shor segem sha narla nultlokh vun dris merdo drelaes rikhga. rir lon mime draemgu vun tin kraek shor tlikh. shor tlisla krir saentaer dishin shor de raekrok.

Pronunciation: [l-ee] [l-ah-l-r-ee] [sh-oh-r] [tl-ee-s-l-ah] [r-oo-r] [sh-oh-r] [s-eh-g-eh-m] [ts-ee-m-oh-n] [g-eye-kh] [kh-eh-kh-n-ee-l] [m-eh-l-m-oh-m] [sh-oh-r] [dr-eh-m] [dr-eh-l-eye-s] [sh-eh-kh-r-eye-s]. [sh-oh-r] [s-eh-g-eh-m] [sh-ah] [n-ah-r-l-ah] [n-oo-l-tl-oh-kh] [v-oo-n] [dr-ee-s] [m-eh-r-d-oh] [dr-eh-l-eye-s] [r-ee-kh-g-ah]. ## Paragraph 4

## Paragraph 6

English: Two friends met at a small café after work. One of them asked how the new job was going. The other explained that it was challenging but exciting. They spent the next hour sharing stories and making weekend plans.

Concilium: shitli tlaerlu kram drin sheslukh nir khikh é morno krur. midra tlunta khekhnil rur shirer shor maesshu valkrar drelaes mikhsho. shor shaer nurshon dak merdo drelaes tonno drenar rikre. rir vis shor tsimon shaekrin vi mendu vun vaemdol khaekhnas drir.

Pronunciation: [sh-ee-tl-ee] [tl-eye-r-l-oo] [kr-ah-m] [dr-ee-n] [sh-eh-s-l-oo-kh] [n-ee-r] [kh-ee-kh] é [m-oh-r-n-oh] [kr-oo-r]. ## Paragraph 7

English: A father asked his daughter how school was today. She explained that her class worked on a science project. He listened carefully and asked a few curious questions. The conversation continued while they prepared dinner together.

Concilium: sheslukh delsho rur drunshir shikhlaen shirer naekhshaer drelaes shishes. mendi nurshon dak tlalrael ne shumo lalri sheslukh rokh dune. lukh kras tla vun rur sheslukh muro nana rel. shor lor krir drernem rir nirra guslon tlael.

Pronunciation: [sh-eh-s-l-oo-kh] [d-eh-l-sh-oh] [r-oo-r] [dr-oo-n-sh-ee-r] [sh-ee-kh-l-eye-n] [sh-ee-r-eh-r] [n-eye-kh-sh-eye-r] [dr-eh-l-eye-s] [sh-ee-sh-eh-s]. ## Paragraph 9

English: Two people met for the first time at a quiet restaurant. They began with simple questions about work and hobbies. Soon the conversation became relaxed and natural. By the end of the evening they agreed to meet again.

Concilium: shitli shaedri kram leskrel shor kherva tokh drin sheslukh kral lem. rir lerer daes moru rel te krur vun nan. gemkha shor lor remdrim shemno vun khordor. ta shor khedra tlunta shor draeno rir linme gaekh tlon naener.

Pronunciation: [sh-ee-tl-ee] [sh-eye-dr-ee] [kr-ah-m] [l-eh-s-kr-eh-l] [sh-oh-r] [kh-eh-r-v-ah] [t-oh-kh] [dr-ee-n] [sh-eh-s-l-oo-kh] [kr-ah-l] [l-eh-m]. ## Paragraph 10

English: A traveler asked a stranger for directions to the train station. The stranger explained the route carefully. The traveler repeated the instructions to make sure they understood. They thanked each other before walking away.

Concilium: sheslukh mamaes rur sheslukh tlarshon leskrel tlaelgo gaekh shor lashaekh shelmil. shor tlarshon nurshon shor khor tla. shor mamaes sher shor dimdraen gaekh shin tas rir khi. rir tasshaekh khos shaer khelda lishon ludos.

Pronunciation: [sh-eh-s-l-oo-kh] [m-ah-m-eye-s] [r-oo-r] [sh-eh-s-l-oo-kh] [tl-ah-r-sh-oh-n] [l-eh-s-kr-eh-l] [tl-eye-l-g-oh] [g-eye-kh] [sh-oh-r] [l-ah-sh-eye-kh] [sh-eh-l-m-ee-l]. ## Paragraph 11

English: A group of friends discussed which movie to watch. Everyone had a different opinion about what sounded interesting. After some debate they agreed to pick something none of them had seen before. The decision took longer than the movie itself.

Concilium: sheslukh tsektsikh tlunta tlaerlu khinsho raekh doslal gaekh kren. kramon shol sheslukh munshokh khal te sho dan gi. morno krenrikh dur rir linme gaekh draetler shuntsim vin tlunta khekhnil shol drarus khelda. shor kri shen shon mil shor doslal lelgaen.

Pronunciation: [sh-eh-s-l-oo-kh] [ts-eh-k-ts-ee-kh] [tl-oo-n-t-ah] [tl-eye-r-l-oo] [kh-ee-n-sh-oh] [r-eye-kh] [d-oh-s-l-ah-l] [g-eye-kh] [kr-eh-n]. ## Paragraph 12

## Paragraph 16

English: Digital platforms allow people to collaborate across the world. Over time these processes influence society in subtle ways. Over time these processes influence society in subtle ways.
